accountable survey system <br>\n     Our system is e.g., used in the <a href=\"https://brave.com/\">Brave</a>\n     browser (founded by Mozilla co-founder Brendan <span class=\"SpellE\">Eich</span>)\n     to enable large-scale anonymous and accountable collection of browsing\n     statistics, with 5.5M monthly users (in Jan 2019).<o:p></o:p></span></li>\n</ul>\n\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\"><b
